<div id="review_1777476171" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1777476171" />
    <a title="♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/52207144"><img alt="♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1568965358p2/52207144.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1777476171?book_show_action=true">Oct 06, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ" href="/user/show/52207144">♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/42606407-a-torch-against-the-night">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=2016-reading-challenge">2016-reading-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=2018-reading-challenge">2018-reading-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=finished-buddy-read">finished-buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=dystopia-and-utopian">dystopia-and-utopian</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1777476171" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8125895797037462193"><u>5 Ten Bleeding Hells STAR'S</u> <br/><br/><i>"But you... are no swift-burning spark. You are a torch against the night – if you dare to let yourself burn."</i><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1526935049i/25576647._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>“Failure doesn't define you. It's what you do after you fail that determines whether you are a leader or a waste of perfectly good air.”</i><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453250960i/17803481._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> Buddy read with my VK/GR besttie <a href='https://www.goodreads.com' rel='nofollow noopener'>Tania Parvin</a><br/><br/>*Reread*<br/>Simply AMAZING!!! Everything about 'A Torch Against the Night' was done so masterfully! It has everything that makes a book great and I couldn't love it more. From the plot</span>
  <span id="freeText8125895797037462193" style="display:none"><u>5 Ten Bleeding Hells STAR'S</u> <br><br><i>"But you... are no swift-burning spark. You are a torch against the night – if you dare to let yourself burn."</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1526935049i/25576647._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>“Failure doesn't define you. It's what you do after you fail that determines whether you are a leader or a waste of perfectly good air.”</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453250960i/17803481._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> Buddy read with my VK/GR besttie <a href="https://www.goodreads.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Tania Parvin</a><br><br>*Reread*<br>Simply AMAZING!!! Everything about 'A Torch Against the Night' was done so masterfully! It has everything that makes a book great and I couldn't love it more. From the plot to the writing, to the world-building and to the characters, everything was so incredibly thought out and Sabaa Tahir takes us on one hell of a journey :D I loved having POV's from Laia, Elias, and Helene. This series has such strong characters, you easily fall in love with them and hope for there happiness. My heart was broken so many times throughout 😭. I loveee Elias so much, he is EVERYTHING! I really enjoy the darkness and brutality of this world. <i>A Torch Against the Night</i> had me completely captivated from the very first page! There is a certain “eeriness” to it that makes it very alluring. This is one of my favorite series and I am never left disappointed! So yeah, that alone says a lot!! I am utterly addicted and obsessed with this beautifully dark and mysterious universe! I <b>CAN'T</b> freaking wait until next month!! I'm dying to read A Reaper at the Gates (#3). I'm getting more and more excited!<br><br><b>*Another beautifully done cover!!! And that title is just perfect!*</b> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1525979309i/25519070._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>“Laia is curled in a ball on the other, one hand on her armlet, fast asleep. <br>"You are my temple", I murmur as I kneel beside her. "You are my priest. You are my prayer. You are my release."- Elias”</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1526935049ra/25576648.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2083088052?book_show_action=true">Aug 09, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25591568-a-torch-against-the-night">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=shocking-twists">shocking-twists</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=forbidden-romance">forbidden-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=dangerous-hero-themed-books-read">dangerous-hero-themed-books-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=love-triangles">love-triangles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=kidnapped">kidnapped</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2083088052" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6542072229312201843">Picking up where 'An Ember in the Ashes' left off, 'A Torch Against the Night' proved to be every bit as suspenseful and action-packed as the first book. Laia and Elias find themselves fighting to survive, as they try and evade the cruelty of the Commandant and the new emperor. There was never a dull moment.<br/><br/>One thing that you should know going into this series is that the author isn't afraid to kill off characters. There were several surprising deaths along the way. Don't be surprised if some of</span>
  <span id="freeText6542072229312201843" style="display:none">Picking up where 'An Ember in the Ashes' left off, 'A Torch Against the Night' proved to be every bit as suspenseful and action-packed as the first book. Laia and Elias find themselves fighting to survive, as they try and evade the cruelty of the Commandant and the new emperor. There was never a dull moment.<br /><br />One thing that you should know going into this series is that the author isn't afraid to kill off characters. There were several surprising deaths along the way. Don't be surprised if some of your favorite characters get nixed along the way. As a result, there is a constant feeling of uncertainty. I was afraid to get too attached, fearing that I'd risk an emotional meltdown in the upcoming chapters.<br /><br />This second book provided a deeper look into the events that led up to the rise of the Martial Empire. The details were very enlightening and cast a different light on current events. It became clear that there were far more players and influences than were previously known.<br /><br />As more and more of the backstory was revealed, I began to realize that things were not what they seemed. Friendships are put to the test. The true enemies are not always obvious. Secret alliances and betrayals kept me guessing the entire time, while supernatural influences became more prominent.<br /><br />Even though I still have a million questions, I enjoyed this book immensely. I cannot wait until the next installment to see how things work out for Elias and Laia. I'm crossing my fingers and hoping that things will heat up a little, because I'm dying for some romance. Nonetheless, I'm loving this series!<br /><br />Check out more of my reviews at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.bookaddicthaven.com">www.bookaddicthaven.com</a></span>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer15076884206430480373">Well I wasn't planning on finishing this book tonight but here we are. This is the only book in a while that has kept me reading past my bedtime because I just needed to FINISH!<br/>I really enjoyed ember when I read it but I think the hype got to me a bit too much and I didn't LOVE it. Not the case with this one. I. LOVE. THIS. BOOK. I was also not 100% on board with it becoming a 4 book series at first (I love duologies! I want more of them!) but after this book I so am. I need more. There is so mu</span>
  <span id="freeText15076884206430480373" style="display:none">Well I wasn't planning on finishing this book tonight but here we are. This is the only book in a while that has kept me reading past my bedtime because I just needed to FINISH!<br />I really enjoyed ember when I read it but I think the hype got to me a bit too much and I didn't LOVE it. Not the case with this one. I. LOVE. THIS. BOOK. I was also not 100% on board with it becoming a 4 book series at first (I love duologies! I want more of them!) but after this book I so am. I need more. There is so much more to exPLORE! I just hope it all connects well and isn't rushed and doesn't feel tacked on.<br />The world building in this book was so much better than book 1, probably because you see more of it. The characters got a lot more fleshed out, especially Helene, and I'm so glad they did.<br />The plot was great, albeit slow at times, but that's my only complaint and it is a very small one.<br />It was just a really good sequel and great setup for more books. </span>

<div id="review_1343894758" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1343894758" />
    <a title="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44137919-mikee-readwithmikee"><img alt="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583262285p2/44137919.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1343894758?book_show_action=true">Jul 24, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" href="/user/show/44137919-mikee-readwithmikee">Mikee (ReadWithMikee)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1343894758" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8787584344804967789"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472970645i/20372438._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Find me on <a href='http://www.instagram.com/readwithmikee' rel='nofollow noopener'>Instagram</a> & <a href='http://www.twitter.com/readwithmikee' rel='nofollow noopener'>Twitter</a>!<br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>❝You are a torch against the night — if you dare to let yourself burn.❞</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>I'm a little undecided on how I feel about A Torch Against the Night. I really liked it but at the same time I wasn't blown away by it...? I guess to put it simply, it was good but nowhere near as good as An Ember in the Ashes. Or maybe I was just expecting too much. I'm not too sure.<br/><br/>I loved some parts and some of the things I wanted to happen DID happen but other parts left me a lit</span>
  <span id="freeText8787584344804967789" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472970645i/20372438._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Find me on <a href="http://www.instagram.com/readwithmikee" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> &amp; <a href="http://www.twitter.com/readwithmikee" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a>!<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>❝You are a torch against the night — if you dare to let yourself burn.❞</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I'm a little undecided on how I feel about A Torch Against the Night. I really liked it but at the same time I wasn't blown away by it...? I guess to put it simply, it was good but nowhere near as good as An Ember in the Ashes. Or maybe I was just expecting too much. I'm not too sure.<br><br>I loved some parts and some of the things I wanted to happen DID happen but other parts left me a little bored and unsatisfied. When I saw that Helene would be getting her own POV, I was ecstatic! I mean what more could I really ask for? But to be honest, I was probably bored with Helene's chapters the most. I found myself... not really caring and sped read through her POVs throughout the whole book. It's like I was interested in what was happening with her storyline and with the Empire but I didn't want to hear this story yet. I kept wanting to go back to Elias and Laia's chapters because that was the story I wanted to keep reading about. I've been waiting for Darin to be rescued since Ember and after that cliffhanger, I just wanted to get a move on! I loved Helene in Ember and I love her even more now as her character continues to evolve. I know many readers will enjoy Helene's POVs but personally, I just wanted to get back to Darin's rescue mission.<br><br>As for Elias and the Soul Catcher, I was a little hesitant at first going into that storyline because I wasn't really sure how it fits into the big picture but I slowly began to grew accustomed to it. I was really intrigued by the magic and how it all worked, and I really can't wait to learn about it in the next book.<br><br>I really enjoyed Laia's development in this book. She's definitely not the same girl we first met in the beginning of Ember! And I was never a huge fan of her and Keenan, and I still wasn't in Torch but I LOVED the storyline between them in general. Well, actually I just love Keenan as a character. And KEENAN. Oh man. I love him but I hate him. I feel bad but I'm like BOY YOU DESERVE IT. That is all I'm going to say.<br><br>In terms of the romance in this book, I'm 100 percent on the Elias/Laia ship since before I even picked up the first book. I've been wanting them to happen and I suppose they do. Kinda. Not quite there yet. So... that left me feeling a little unsatisfied lol. The tension has always been there and as much as I hate instalove, this slow-burn romance is KILLING ME. Lord have mercy on my poor soul because I can't handle another book without my ship officially happening.<br><br>OKAY. This book was far from perfect but I had one specific issue that left me absolutely fuming. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[IZZI. Why in ten hells would you do this to us Sabaa??? Was that really necessary!? Izzi was such an amazing character. She did NOT deserve to be killed off like that or even at all! -___- All because she was trying to protect Gibran. None of us probably gives two shits about Gibran and yet Gibran lives for the price of Izzi. Not cool at all. Izzi deserved more than that. She didn't even NEED to die. She was pointlessly killed off and I couldn't be any more upset by this. SHE DID NOT HAVE TO DIE. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> This issue alone would've been enough to dock off a whole star because it's honestly so upsetting...<br><br>Overall, I liked Torch but I didn't love it. The pacing was a little slow in a lot of parts and I didn't really enjoy Helene's chapters as much as I hoped to, but this was still a fairly good follow up to An Ember in the Ashes. I was expecting a little more from this book because the story I was actually hoping to read happens on the very last page but I guess that just means that the next book will be even better. Hopefully!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="8787584344804967789" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6511257-sue-hollywood-news-source?shelf=authors-of-color">authors-of-color</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6511257-sue-hollywood-news-source?shelf=diverse-books">diverse-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6511257-sue-hollywood-news-source?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6511257-sue-hollywood-news-source?shelf=characters-of-color">characters-of-color</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1283772748" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10549157986293098934"><strong>
  <br/>
</strong>A Torch Against the Night is simply the superior YA Fantasy of the year. Hands down, there's no competition.<br/><em>
  <br/>
</em>An Ember in the Ashes was merely a prelude to the sinister follow up. The story remains about oppression, but unlike the first book this is where readers could vividly see the resistance at first hand. The stakes are higher. There is more gore, and violence.<br/><br/>My heart is very delighted with the intricate political prose, but there are truths in it as well that parallels our past and </span>
  <span id="freeText10549157986293098934" style="display:none"><strong>
  <br />
</strong>A Torch Against the Night is simply the superior YA Fantasy of the year. Hands down, there's no competition.<br /><em>
  <br />
</em>An Ember in the Ashes was merely a prelude to the sinister follow up. The story remains about oppression, but unlike the first book this is where readers could vividly see the resistance at first hand. The stakes are higher. There is more gore, and violence.<br /><br />My heart is very delighted with the intricate political prose, but there are truths in it as well that parallels our past and contemporary times.<br /><br />There are scenes that would undoubtedly take a dig at your heart such as this:<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <em> I look to the little boy in his arms. Ayan. Tiny dark crescents curve beneath his lower lashes. His eyes meet mine, and I touch his cheek, soft and round. He should be innocent. But he’s seen things no child should. Who will he be when he grows up? What will all this violence make him? Will he survive? Not another forgotten child with a forgotten name, I plead. Not another lost Scholar. </em>
</blockquote><br /><em> </em><br /><br /> 
  <strong>Characters</strong>
 <br /><br /><strong>If it’s a story of war, it’s going to be a story of survival as well. A Torch Against the Night touches that, but truly, the heart of the story is the girl who dared and the boy who rejected his destiny that is built on systematic oppression. </strong> <br /><br />We have a tyrannical emperor who is beyond ruthless, and a commandant who is also beyond salvation.<br /><br /><strong>Let’s talk about Helene Aquilla’s dangerous feminism.</strong><br /><br />I could understand the allure of her character. She’s a woman who carved a path for herself in an environment that undermine women. She’s a sword-wielding soldier, loyal to the empire-to her duty, family, and Elias. But, her firm stance on Scholars are threaded with racism and classism. This is very important, since I’m getting the vibes the narrative is brushing it off under the rug. This is not the first time she made an offhand comment about the oppression of the slaves. She made countless of remarks on book one as well.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <em>“Didn’t the Scholar rebels understand what they would unleash when they revolted? Didn’t they realize the death and terror the Empire would rain down upon them?</em>
</blockquote><br /><blockquote>
  <em>“I’ve never seen the Scholars as enemies, exactly. An enemy is someone you fear. Someone who might destroy you. But the Scholars will never destroy the Martials. They can’t read. They have no steelcraft. They are a slave class-a lesser class.”</em>
</blockquote><br />If there’s one thing I got from Helene’s character is she thinks the martials are the superior race than the Scholars and the tribal people. To her Scholars, who are canonically brown people, who has been enslaved and systematically murdered on their own land are subhuman. For Helene, they should merely accept their destiny as slaves. To her, they don’t deserve to uproot their lives and dream. This is what makes Elias and Helene different. Elias with his given maternal’s privilege and station, he saw through everything. His eyes are wide open and conscious with the imperialism that is going on around him. Like Helene, he was brainwashed by the empire too; but he stopped himself before he become a harbinger of destruction. Helene had that chance. He showed her the terrifying lives of the Scholars. She chose not to be moved.<br /><br />To me her “empowering” arc isn’t truly empowering. She might be powerless and marginalized when she’s surrounded by the Martials, but she has her white-empire cloak that protects her. Helene’s suffering is nothing significant compared to the ethnic cleansing of Scholars. I want everyone to remember that.<br /><br />I’m in awe of Laia and her strength. She’s a fun character to read. She grows and learn from her mistakes. We should revolutionize that.<br /><br /> 
  <strong>Romance</strong>
 <br /><br />The romance didn’t take over the plot. <em>(sad face) </em>It was barely<em> there. </em>Though, it was enough to keep me going. Who would ever have thought Elias is romantic at heart?!? Who noticed those suggestive metaphors? I am swooning.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <em>“You are my temple,” I murmur as I kneel beside her. “You are my priest. You are my prayer. You are my release.”</em>
</blockquote><br /><br />If you’re on the fence about picking it up, you <em>still s</em>hould consider. There are lovely resurfacing characters, women that doesn’t need protecting, tight knit friendship and family dynamics. It’s basically my wet dream.<br /><br /><strong>Without doubt, A Torch Against the Night is a revelation and revolution. Given the political climate right now, this story is more relevant than ever.</strong><br /><br />Review also posted at Amazon and <a href="http://hollywoodnewssource.com/hns-book-review-a-torch-against-the-night-an-ember-in-the-ashes-2-by-sabaa-tahir" rel="nofollow noopener">Hollywood News Source</a>. </span>
  <a data-text-id="10549157986293098934" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1283766677" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3961205094691705396">OH MY GOD.<br/>Did I ever think Sabaa Tahir would let me down? Because if any part of me did, swiftly punch it to non-existence. Thanks.<br/><br/>I'm literally on the floor crying yet my heart feels so full.<br/><br/><i>An Ember in The Ashes</i> lingered on suspense and brutality. The stakes have been high since the beginning. <i>A Torch Against the Night</i> is even more brutal, more heart racing and oh yeah, lots more deaths and twists that really had me worried for my heart. <br/><br/>The pacing is different to that of <i>AEITA</i> because there's</span>
  <span id="freeText3961205094691705396" style="display:none">OH MY GOD.<br>Did I ever think Sabaa Tahir would let me down? Because if any part of me did, swiftly punch it to non-existence. Thanks.<br><br>I'm literally on the floor crying yet my heart feels so full.<br><br><i>An Ember in The Ashes</i> lingered on suspense and brutality. The stakes have been high since the beginning. <i>A Torch Against the Night</i> is even more brutal, more heart racing and oh yeah, lots more deaths and twists that really had me worried for my heart. <br><br>The pacing is different to that of <i>AEITA</i> because there's no trials of course. You could consider this a travelling adventure with lots of show downs. There's no lack of heart palpitating scenes and even heart breaking ones. My favourite part of this book was the exploration of the Martials, the scholars, the tribes and the fantastical beings. The different facets of this world actually make you understand the Empire and it's importance.<br><br>I love Elias, Helena and Laia with all my heart. Each character has a different perspective, a different story to tell in this world. They're so much more than a romantic connection and that is clearly evident by the end of this book.<br><b>Laia</b> really grows into a spark of hope in this sequel. Her emotions and character really touched me and I found myself rooting for her even more than I was before. <br><b>Helene</b>, my one true love, my heart broke for her and she also broke mine a couple of times. Helene is the most complex character but not from a lack of understanding mind you. You understand her every motive and every emotion and that's how Sabaa Tahir weaves her tangled webs.<br>And finally, <b>Elias</b>. My heart ached for him since the beginning of this book and it's aching still. Make of that what you wish. I just love him with all my heart and I need a better fate for him plz Sabaa pleeeeeaaaaaseeeee.<br><br>I can't wait for the next book. I need it now.<br>-------------<br><b>Before reading</b><br>THANK YOU PENGUIN AND SABAA FOR THIS BLESSING.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431996830ra/14891707.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>Now the wait begins. ELIAS I WILL WAIT FOR YOU.</span>

<div id="review_1747491593" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1747491593" />
    <a title="Simona B" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5312173-simona-b"><img alt="Simona B" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1408893128p2/5312173.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1747491593?book_show_action=true">Sep 03, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Simona B" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Simona B" href="/user/show/5312173-simona-b">Simona B</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5312173-simona-b?shelf=fantastic-lit-and-co">fantastic-lit-and-co</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5312173-simona-b?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5312173-simona-b?shelf=2000">2000</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5312173-simona-b?shelf=in-english">in-english</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1747491593" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11001116174690875390">*Fellow readers, please, for your own good, go read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1285100011' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kat's</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1614771595' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sarah's</a>, and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1310758788' rel='nofollow noopener'>Nastassya's</a> reviews- I just did it, and I know I will be laughing for hours. Besides, you know I always mention them, and I don't do it only because we discuss the book together: it's because they know what it means to review a book and analyze it with humor and intellectual honesty. I was almost cut out from the world for the past week and the only reason I wanted to leave the wonderful place I'd gone on vacation to was to </span>
  <span id="freeText11001116174690875390" style="display:none">*Fellow readers, please, for your own good, go read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1285100011" rel="nofollow noopener">Kat's</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1614771595" rel="nofollow noopener">Sarah's</a>, and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1310758788" rel="nofollow noopener">Nastassya's</a> reviews- I just did it, and I know I will be laughing for hours. Besides, you know I always mention them, and I don't do it only because we discuss the book together: it's because they know what it means to review a book and analyze it with humor and intellectual honesty. I was almost cut out from the world for the past week and the only reason I wanted to leave the wonderful place I'd gone on vacation to was to read their opinions with my leisure. Turns out it really was worth the wait. And I also recommend, just as enthusiastically, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1463144457" rel="nofollow noopener">Minni's review</a>, because I'm just speechless. These are all professionals' reviews, my friends. (So, yes, no need for you to bother with mine.)<br /><br />---<br /><br />Ladies and gentlemen, mesdams et messieurs, signore e signori, I welcome you to the cliché fair –with quotes.<br /><br />•<b>"The poor little boy getting vengeance for his lost youth. Pathetic, Elias."</b><br /><br />I almost feel like this is too low a blow. Just read “redemption” instead of “vengeance” (I daresay it’s even <i>more</i> pathetic) and you have the truth about Elias. He is the king of clichés: repented soldier, insta-love stricken young Adonis, volunteered martyr. There is nothing, absolutely nothing about him that can be considered unexpected or unpredictable, nothing that isn’t perfectly in line with the type of person it was at the beginning of book one. Not even his fate at the end of this book could surprise or thrill me, probably because it felt like a random choice. (I am convinced that I had this impression due to the lacking world building. I’ll get to it.)<br /><br />•<b>“We can’t just leave them.”</b><br /><br />Laia, sweetie, if your own neck is on stake and there’s absolutely nothing you can do to help those poor people you don’t even know personally, like hell you can. I think no one would ever dare judge you on that. Stop being such a freaking bleeding heart.<br /><br />Which leads me to one of the immediately apparent flaws of this series: the <b>lack of progress in the character development</b>. After everything these characters have been through, it would be normal (it would be <i>essential</i>) for the reader to perceive how they have have grown, how their experiences changed their minds and spirits. In fact, however Tahir’s character development is so weak and <b>defective</b>, I don’t think I would have noticed if the personality of any of the characters had underwent any change that didn’t concern who loves who, Laia’s do-goodism or Elias self-centered desire for redemption. <br /><br />But while it’s true that<b> Elias and Laia are inexcusably static</b>, the third main character, <b>Helene</b>, <b>gave me more food for thought</b>. She is deeply torn between her due loyalty to her family and the Empire and the strong relationship that binds her to Elias, and from the very beginning she resolves to act according to the obligations of the first. Since she’s but a human being, she questions her decision again and again. I totally agree with the author’s choice to give Helene doubts about her doing, since seeing how strong Helene’s attachment to Elias and her loyalty to the Empire were, any other path for her would have felt like a bit out-of-character. The thing is that <b>Tahir does not know how to give a character its due depth</b>. Helene is complex only on the surface: deep down, she’s flat as paper, just like the others. She is the only interesting character of this book, and I could not care for her less than what she does.<br />In my review of book one, I said the Commander was the one character worthy of notice. I apologize for myself: she is only stereotypical and caricatural, and the same description may be applied to all the secondary characters of the series, none excluded. I don’t know if she was so in <i>An Ember in the Ashes</i> as well and I simply didn’t see it, or if in fact she is different in <i>A Torch Against the Night</i>, but she is. She’s evil <i>inside</i>. End of characterization. <br /><br />•<b>
  <i>"Disappear, Laia."</i>
</b><br /><br />Yes, the truth about Laia’s power: she can read minds. In this case, she read mine.<br />Another of my perplexities about Laia’s character is linked to her supposed powers and, more generally, to <b>the world building</b>. I am of the opinion that explaining half of what the fuss is about to create suspense and explaining nothing at all are two very different things. Hint for the aspiring authors out there: the first is good (if you know how to do it) the second is bad (even if you think you know how to do it). Why? Basically, because since I haven’t got the littlest clue regarding why on earth Laia is turning into a special snowflake, I just perceive it as the most random thing I’ve ever read. Sorry not sorry. <br /><br />And now, what everyone was waiting for (except me. I’d actually like to be able to erase all this shit from my mind.): <b>the romance</b>.<br /><br />•<b>"My hands are filled with her-waist, hips, that cloud of sugar-scented hair."</b><br /><br />After days and days of travel through forests and deserts, I wouldn’t bet Laia’s hair smelled like sugar if she had a cotton candy machine implanted beneath her scalp. Maybe she magicked Elias’s scent receptors into a stupor.<br /><br />•<b>“Was it … wrong?”<br /> “To find an hour or two of bliss in such dark times?” Keenan says. “That’s not wrong.”</b><br /><br />What’s wrong, Laia, is that, as I’ve previously said and repeated ad nauseam, you are a goldfish whose memory resets itself every 30 seconds. Keenan’s not here, let’s hit on Elias; Elias’s not here, let’s have fun with Keenan. I cannot second this behavior. What’s worse, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[she throws herself in Keenan’s arms because Elias keeps his distance because of the poison that’s slowly killing him, even though she is not sure she really loves Keenan <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I see that she probably needed a shoulder to cry on, and if she wanted to <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[have sex with him <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, she can help herself, but spare me the “I love him. Don’t I?” rigmarole later. It’s pathetic and unnecessary. <br /><br />•<b>“You are my temple,” I murmur as I kneel beside her. “You are my priest. You are my prayer. You are my release.”</b><br /><br />I keep being insensitive and simply not seeing where this declaration comes from. It still felt as if they knew <i>nothing</i> about each other, and their chemistry is so non existent the only fire I felt was in my head- my brain cells imploding. <br /><br />➽ I am 90% sure I won’t continue the series. <i>A Torch Against the Night</i> was downright embarrassing. I would rate it one star, but I reserve the single star to books I find offensive or excessively badly written even for my obstinacy, and I think this book is neither of those things, but<b> I personally found it tasteless and worthless</b>. It had potential, no doubt, but oh, if it was wasted. If it was wasted.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11001116174690875390" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2227107384" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2227107384" />
    <a title="Beth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44125660-beth"><img alt="Beth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600268807p2/44125660.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2227107384?book_show_action=true">Dec 26, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beth" href="/user/show/44125660-beth">Beth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780008160340" href="/book/show/25716704-a-torch-against-the-night">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=faves">faves</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=swoony-swoony">swoony-swoony</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=book-series">book-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=my-heart-hurts">my-heart-hurts</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=characters-i-loved">characters-i-loved</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2227107384" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16882042536376259097"><i>Spoiler Free Review.</i>... I've now added to this review and it's only at the very end there will be spoilers (which is marked in capitals and in bold, so here is your warning)<br/><br/><b>ALL OF THE STARS!</b><br/><br/><i>”Don’t lock yourself away from those who care about you because you think you’ll hurt them or - or they’ll hurt you. What point is there in being human if you don’t let yourself fell anything?</i><br/><br/>Buddy Read with these lovely ladies!<br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1434563896?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Fathima</a><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2220981290?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Tânia</a><br/><b>We were not ready!</b><br/><br/>Where to even begin with this review… After reading </span>
  <span id="freeText16882042536376259097" style="display:none"><i>Spoiler Free Review.</i>... I've now added to this review and it's only at the very end there will be spoilers (which is marked in capitals and in bold, so here is your warning)<br /><br /><b>ALL OF THE STARS!</b><br /><br /><i>”Don’t lock yourself away from those who care about you because you think you’ll hurt them or - or they’ll hurt you. What point is there in being human if you don’t let yourself fell anything?</i><br /><br />Buddy Read with these lovely ladies!<br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1434563896?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Fathima</a><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2220981290?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Tânia</a><br /><b>We were not ready!</b><br /><br />Where to even begin with this review… After reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/27774758.An_Ember_in_the_Ashes__An_Ember_in_the_Ashes___1_" title="An Ember in the Ashes (An Ember in the Ashes, #1) by Sabaa Tahir" rel="nofollow noopener">An Ember in the Ashes</a>, I was so excited to get my hands on this. I can now safely say I was not disappointed in the slightest! This book continues exactly where the first one left off and it was done so beautifully, even within the first few chapters my heart was nearly bursting from my chest at the suspense and worry for all of the characters! We got so much more information in this book that I was <u>NOT</u> ready for! I mean the twists and the turns had me screaming at my book like OH MY GOD! I honestly had to put the book down and just sit there and then message Fathima and Tania being like Can you believe it! <br /><br />We get so many new and intriguing characters brought into this book, not only that but we get the point of view from Helene. Initially in the first book, I wasn’t Helene’s biggest fan, but I liked her so much more in this book and the fact that we can see her thought process makes things so much better! The character progression in this book was done BEAUTIFULLY, we seem the grow and become stronger. Though mistakes are made we see how they learn from them. I think what was so well done, was Elias’s realising of what he should and should not take on as his own. I seriously have all of the heart eyes for Elias I’m not going to beat around the bush here!<br /><br /><u>Characters</u><br /><br /><i>”I know what is to do things that you don’t want to for the greater good."</i><br /><br /><b>Laia</b> develops SO much in this book. When we first see her in AEITA, we see a scared girl who seems to be dependent on others. This time around she really comes into her own and leads others on what to do. We see things begin to emerge and let me tell you now I want MORE! I need these answer! Although things don’t always go to plan, we see how she deals with these things and overall it makes her stronger.<br /><br /><i>"You always think everyone is your responsibility… We;re our own people, and we deserve to make our own decisions.”</i><br /><br />Oh lord. <i>Elias</i>, why am I having heart eyes so much right now? His relationship with The Soul Catcher was so intriguing, and his time at The Waiting Place. It was a really interesting concept and how he figures certain things out. His time there and with certain people nearly ripped my heart into pieces. His relationship with Maime was just ADORABLE, and the fact he took no shit from Afya when collecting, I was like YOU TELL EM’!<br /><br /><i>Loyal to the end.</i><br /><br />We FINALLY got <b>Helene</b> chapters! (hoorahhhh!), I absolutely love strong female characters and Helene is everything! I loved how she figured how to handle certain situations and when it comes to disrespect she has none of it! I liked her friendship with <b>Harper</b>, and even though she is Blood Shrike she listens to the people who know best. I am SO intrigued to find out what is to come of her!<br /><br />For the longest time <i>Keenan</i> was on my radar, he really really wound me up, (not to mention he was messing with my ship!) the reason why he annoyed me so much was that he seemed to undermine everything that Laia would do, and I was having none of that! <br /><br />What <b>I liked?</b><br />- <b>That mother-fucking twist… BAM, BAM, BAMMMMM!</b><br />- I have the biggest soft spot EVER for Tas, like come on, how could I not?! THEN we have Elias consoling him, it was too sweet!<br />- I know I just mentioned Tas, but when he slapped Elias and was like You named me, I want to hear my name on other peoples lips I was SCREAMING<br />- Maime! Her speech was riveting and I got goosebumps e’rywhereeeee<br />- I am a sucker for evil type characters, we have so many in this: Marcus, The Commandant, The Nightbringer and The Warden we have such a sense of <i>Good vs Evil</i> and I love it<br />- I need more cook!<br />- ALL OF THE HEARTBREAK! <br />- Afya, I need you in my life more pleaseeeee<br />- Izzi literally doesn’t miss a thing!<br /><br />What <b>didn’t I like?</b><br />- The only thing that put me off with this was the pacing of the book, at times it felt slightly scattered, things seem to move very very quickly but not always making sense. <br /><br />Overall, I can truly say this is becoming a much loved series of mine, I’m enjoying all aspects and the characters are so well done, I need more and I’m really really looking forward to reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/30809786.A_Reaper_at_the_Gates__An_Ember_in_the_Ashes___3_" title="A Reaper at the Gates (An Ember in the Ashes, #3) by Sabaa Tahir" rel="nofollow noopener">A Reaper at the Gates</a>. It's a good job I pre-ordered on Amazon. However I have different dates coming up so if someone wants to let me know when it will officially be released I will love you forever!<br /><br /><i>"Failure doesn’t define you. It’s what you do after you fail that determines whether you are a leader or a waste of perfectly good air.”</i><br /><br />---------<br /> <br />After thought ramble...<br /><br />THIS. I love this so much. This is slowly becoming a well loved series, like one of my favourites...<br />I have so many questions, I need to know things!<br /><br />What an absolute rollercoaster of a ride, I was up and down and up again, all of the curveballs, the DECEIT! <br />I NEED MORE!<br /><br />Is my ship sailing?!<br />Who's in the next book?!<br />What is going to happen?!<br />--------<br /><br /><b>SPOILERS AHEAD</b><br /><br />19.10.2019<br />I still love this series, love all of my favourite characters, but I have so much I want to say. My main thing/person I want to talk about is Keenan. During my re-read I noticed so many little things leading up to the big reveal, and I'm honestly stunned that I didn't even realise. The manipulation used throughout was SO subtle and each time I noticed it I'd be screaming into my book.<br /><br />I'm just going to point out I still absolutely love the majority of the characters and each re-read fills me with so much love. Going into this I had a lot of knowledge of what happens in Reaper At The Gates, and there are so many subtle hints of what's to come.<br /><br />07.07.2020<br /><br />1. I still love Elias<br />2. My girl Hel goes through SO much shit, and just thinking about my re-read of Reaper I’m already dreading so much<br />3. Laia... WHYYYYYYYY U DO DIS<br />4. I hate Keenan, The Commandant, Marcus...<br />5. I love Harper.<br /><br />Elias Veturius, you are a complete and utter babe.<br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2201576087?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">An Ember in the Ashes</a> - 5 Stars<br />A Torch Against the Night - 5 Stars<br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2227113693" rel="nofollow noopener">A Reaper at the Gates</a> - 5 Stars</span>
  <a data-text-id="16882042536376259097" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1476478209" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1476478209" />
    <a title="Jaclyn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3015778-jaclyn"><img alt="Jaclyn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1389758695p2/3015778.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1476478209?book_show_action=true">Dec 22, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jaclyn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jaclyn" href="/user/show/3015778-jaclyn">Jaclyn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1476478209" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11572852706688680895"><b> 5 BIG BRIGHT BLAZING STARS FOR THIS ONE! </b> <br/><br/><b> <i> So long as you fight the darkness, you stand in the light. </i></b>  <br/><br/><i> GUYS </i> <br/><br/>THIS BOOK!!!!!! GET HYPED BECAUSE ITS A FANTASTIC SEQUEL!! AHHHHH!!!<br/><br/>THANK YOU SO MUCH PENGUIN FOR SENDING THIS TO ME! <br/><br/>*deep breathes*<br/><br/>Okay let's start from the beginning..<br/><br/><s> <i> let me list my feels </i></s>  <br/><br/>This one picks up right where we left off with Elias and Laia running for their lives from Blackcliff. They're on the run with nowhere to go, just this mission of breaking Laia's brother out f</span>
  <span id="freeText11572852706688680895" style="display:none"><b> 5 BIG BRIGHT BLAZING STARS FOR THIS ONE! </b> <br /><br /><b> <i> So long as you fight the darkness, you stand in the light. </i></b>  <br /><br /><i> GUYS </i> <br /><br />THIS BOOK!!!!!! GET HYPED BECAUSE ITS A FANTASTIC SEQUEL!! AHHHHH!!!<br /><br />THANK YOU SO MUCH PENGUIN FOR SENDING THIS TO ME! <br /><br />*deep breathes*<br /><br />Okay let's start from the beginning..<br /><br /><s> <i> let me list my feels </i></s>  <br /><br />This one picks up right where we left off with Elias and Laia running for their lives from Blackcliff. They're on the run with nowhere to go, just this mission of breaking Laia's brother out from Kauf, a highly secured and terrifying prison. They have enemies chasing them from a multiple different directions and things are VERY INTENSE AND SUPER NERVEWRACKING. <br /><br /><b> <i> Perhaps grief is like a battle: After experiencing enough of, your body's instincts take over. When you see it closing in like a Martial death squad, you harden your insides. You prepare for the agony of a shredded heart. And when it hits, it hurts, but not as badly, because you have locked away your weakness, and all that's left is anger and strength. </i></b>  <br /><br />It was heart stopping, breathless, riveting, and addicting to read. The stakes are so much higher in than the first one. Life, love and death loom just around the corner of every page. It was so hard to put down, and so easy to just sit and read as the hours ticked away and disappeared completely. I absolutely LOVED this sequel!! So many parts made me SO NERVOUS!!! <br /><br /><b> <i> Defiantly, I edge closer to him. He clenches his jaw but doesn't move. Without looking away, I bring a tentative hand to his mouth. Those lips, curved like they're always smiling, even when his eyes are lit with desire, as they are now. <br />"This is a bad idea," he murmurs. We're so close that I can see a long eyelash that's landed in his cheek. I can see the hints of blue in his hair. <br />"Then why aren't you stopping it?" <br />"Because I'm a fool." We breathe each other's breath, and his body relaxes as his hands finally slide around my back, I close my eyes. <br /></i></b>  <br /><br />There's some romance, heartache, adventure, a SHOCKING plot twist..and then another HUGE plot twist and all of it leads to an epic ending. <br /><br />(BUT REALLY THOSE PLOT TWIST WERE KILLING ME. Seriously some of the biggest twist that I EVER read! Still not over it!!!)<br /><br /><b> <i> Perhaps I have become so accustomed to the burden of secrets that I do not notice their weight until I am free. </i></b> <br /><br />In this book we get three different point of view and it's broken up into four different sections. We follow alternating points of view between Elias, Laia, and Helene. I loved having this constant switch of back and forth. It's such a clever way of storytelling and each chapter would end with a cliffhanger, but then it picks up from someone else's point of view where something completely different is happening, so you need to keep reading and reading until you get back to the other point of view that was driving you crazy. It seriously keeps the reader engaged and eager to learn more just like the first one. Each point of view had a unique voice and it was extremely simple to distinguish between who was who. Such talented writing! The world building was so much better than the first one. In the first book, I struggled to get a good visual of this world but in this one it was so clearly laid out. And it was so MUCH FUN being back in this world!! <br /><br /><b> <i> When you love, there is always more pain. </i></b>  <br /><br />We have two separate storylines going with Elias and Laia on the run and then Helene who is the new Blood Shrike and has been tasked with her first mission: to hunt down and kill Elias, who was her best friend for most of their life. <br /><br /><b> <i> Elias and Laia are each other's countermelodies. I am just a dissonant note. </i></b>  <br /><br />My heart ached for Helene throughout the entire book. In the first one, she was a really frustrating character but in this book, seeing from her point of view it really made me love her! She is so STRONG and kickass! And dedicated to her family! I loved her development from then and now and it was truly one of the highlights for me. <br /><br /><b> <i> "But you, Helene Aquilla, are no swift/burning spark. You are a torch against the night- if you dare to let yourself burn." </i></b>  <br /><br />*slow clap for amazing character development*<br /><br />I loved following her story and watching it interweave with Laia and Elias's story was brilliant!<br /><br /><s> this entire book was brilliant though </s> <br /><br />I loved watching Elias and Laia start to get to know each other better and eventually care for one another. It was so SWEET!!! Elias is so STRONG and some of what he goes through in this book is heartbreaking!!! I'm so in love with him and it was so hard to read some of the things he was going through!! Ahhh!! Elias girls, be prepared!! <br /> <br /><b> <i> ""Look at me." I meet his gaze. The Commandants eyes. No Elias's. "I'm not her," he takes my chin, and while it must look threatening to those watching, his hand is light as a breeze."I won't hurt you. But you can't let the fear take you."" </i></b>  <br /><br />And as for Laia, she became so BRAVE! She's growing more into herself and becoming more secure in what she believes in and for her people. She's so loyal to her brother and it's so touching to see as to what lengths she would go through to get him back. <br /><br /><b> <i> You're emotions make you human. Even the unpleasant ones have a purpose. Don't lock them away. If you ignore them, they just get louder and angrier. </i> </b><br /><br />Honestly, this book blew through all my expectations and is easily one of the best books I've read in 2016. I don't know how I'm supposed to wait AN ENTIRE YEAR FOR THE NEXT ONE!!! Ahhh!!! Until then, I'll just be rereading all of my favorite parts. If you loved, Ember in the Ashes, then get excited because this sequel was PERFECT! If you haven't read An Ember In The Ashes then get on that!!! Such an amazing series!! <br /><br /><b> <i> "I thought you told me you loved stories. Have you ever heard of an adventurer with a sane plan?"<br />"Well..no."<br />"And why do you think that it?"<br />I am at a loss. "Because...ah, because-"<br />She chuckles again. "Because sane plans never work girl," she says. "Only the mad ones do." </i></b>  <br /><br /><br />Thank you again to Penguin!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="11572852706688680895" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('WIHvsbxkASpGYgQcwX/oESRKvntyK4X6GKB4DvOc9H7HDPgbh0WW3b+VVaOhnFqKPxMxnntNmT41+pdTKH9dgQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('G3VfUSQjj7+Lj/lGpNQZPXxJS9K8Apdtl449vNgCg1CE+Ej7HwIYSHJ4qPnEN6umZxDEN7Vki6m61NLhA+Eqrw==')})
  }

But the choice has never been hers.\n\nA Duty…\n\nThe entire kingdom’s future rests on Poppy’s shoulders, something she’s not even quite sure she wants for herself. Because a Maiden has a heart.
